        <script>
        require(['jquery','bnimagemap'], function ($) {
            if($('#bannerslider-list-items-396-605eb20db1b97').length){
                var element = $('#bannerslider-list-items-396-605eb20db1b97').find('img.owl-lazy');
                if(element.length > 0){
                    element.each(function(event){
                        var $this = jQuery(this);
                        var origin_url = $this.data('src');
                        var new_url = '';
                        if (origin_url && origin_url != 'undefined'){
                            if(jQuery(window).width() <= 650 && $this.attr('data-mobiledesc') == 'true'){
                                origin_url = origin_url.replace(/.([^.]*)$/, '_mobile.' + '$1')
                            }
                            new_url = origin_url;
                            $this.attr('src',new_url);
                            $this.removeAttr('data-src');
                        }

                        var attrUseMap = $this.attr('usemap') || false;
                        if (typeof attrUseMap !== typeof undefined && attrUseMap !== false) {
                            if(jQuery(window).width() <= 650){
                                var map = $this.attr('usemap').replace('#', ''),
                                c = 'coords',
                                cMobi = 'coordsmobi';
                                if($this.parent().find('map[name="' + map + '"]').find('area').length){
                                    $this.parent().find('map[name="' + map + '"]').find('area').each(function() {
                                        var _areaThis = jQuery(this);
                                        if (_areaThis.data(cMobi)){
                                            _areaThis.attr(c, _areaThis.data(cMobi));
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                            }
                            $this.bnImageMaps();
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });
    </script>

</div><script type="text/javascript">
    require(['jquery'], function($){
        $( document ).ready(function() {
            $( "body" ).on( "click", ".product-item a", function() {
                var parentItem = $(this).closest('.product-item');
                if(parentItem && parentItem.find('.data_custom_option').length > 0 && parentItem.find('.data_custom_option').attr('data-url'))
                {
                    var url = parentItem.find('.data_custom_option').attr('data-url') + '';
                    var currentUrl = $(this).attr('href');
                    var urls = url.split('?');
                    var currentUrl = currentUrl.split('?');
                    if(url && urls[0] == currentUrl[0]) {
                        $(this).attr('href', url);
                    }
                }
            });
            $('.product-item a:not(.color_product)').each(function (index, value) {
                var parentItem = $(this).closest('.product-item');
                if(parentItem && parentItem.find('.data_custom_option').length > 0 && parentItem.find('.data_custom_option').attr('data-url'))
                {
                    var url = parentItem.find('.data_custom_option').attr('data-url') + '';
                    var currentUrl = $(this).attr('href');
                    var urls = url.split('?');
                    var currentUrl = currentUrl.split('?');
                    if(url && urls[0] == currentUrl[0]) {
                        $(this).attr('href', url);
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    })

  $(function () {
    $(document).on('ftr:customerWebIdReady', function (ev, webId) {

<script type="text/javascript">//<![CDATA[
require(["jquery", "jquery/jquery.cookie"], function(jQuery) {
	jQuery("#showroom-booking-popup .close_icon").on("click", function(){
        var lifetime = 7*24*3600;
        var expireAt = jQuery.mage.cookies.expires;
        expireAt = new Date();
        expireAt.setTime(expireAt.getTime() + lifetime * 1000);
        jQuery.cookie('SHOWROOM_BOOKING_CLOSE', 1, {path: '/', expires: expireAt});
	  	jQuery('#showroom-booking-popup').fadeOut('slow');
	});

	jQuery("#showroom-booking-popup .button").on("click", function(){
	  	jQuery('#showroom-booking-popup').hide();
	}); 

    jQuery(window).load(function() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            if (jQuery.cookie('SHOWROOM_BOOKING_EMAIL')) {
                jQuery('#showroom-booking-popup').hide();
            }else if(jQuery.cookie('SHOWROOM_BOOKING_CLOSE')){
                jQuery('#showroom-booking-popup').hide();
            }else{
                jQuery('#showroom-booking-popup').fadeIn('slow');
            }
        });
    });
});
//]]></script>

<script>
    require([
        'jquery'
    ], function ($) {
        'use strict';
        $(document).ready(function () {
            var body = $('body');
            function showHideElementContent(ele, element_content) {
                var ele = $(ele);
                var content = ele.next(element_content);
                if (ele.hasClass('active')) {
                    ele.removeClass('active');
                    content.removeClass('show');
                } else {
                    ele.addClass('active');
                    content.addClass('show');
                }
            }
            if ($('.geoip-close') && $('#geoip-detect')) {
                $('.geoip-close').click(function() {
                    $('#geoip-detect').hide();
                })
            }
            body.on('click', '.geoip_select_option', function(){
                showHideElementContent('.geoip_select_option','.geoip_select_content');
                var idClass = $('.geoip_select_option .item-option').attr('data-id');

                $('.ip-option').show();
                $('.' + idClass).hide();
            });
            body.on('click', '.ip-option', function(){
                var ip_option = $(this).html();
                $(".geoip_select_option").removeClass('active');
                $(".geoip_select_content").removeClass('show');
                $(".geoip_select_option").html(ip_option);
                var link_other = $(".geoip_select_option label").attr("data-href");
                $(".button-ip a").attr("href",link_other);
            });
        })
    });


</script>

    <script>
        require([
            'jquery',
            'jquery/jquery.cookie'
        ], function ($) {
            if (!$.cookie('cookienotice')) document.getElementById('m-cookienotice').style.display = 'block';
            $('#m-cookienotice .m-accept').on('click',function(){
                cookieNoticeAccept();
                $('#m-cookienotice').hide();
            });
            function cookieNoticeAccept() {
                var lifetime = 365 * 24 * 3600;
                expireAt = new Date();
                expireAt.setTime(expireAt.getTime() + lifetime * 1000);
                $.cookie('cookienotice', 1, {path: '/', expires: expireAt});
            }
        });
    </script>
